      <div id="js-article-text" class="article-text wide  heading-tag-switch">
            <h2>Sickening video from Brazil prison battle shows twisted gang members playing soccer with the decapitated heads of their rivals as 57 are killed in bloody clash</h2><ul class="mol-bullets-with-font"><li class="class"><b>Several inmates were seen goofing off on top of the jail during Monday's riots </b></li><li class="class"><b>They appeared to be using human heads as balls for a twisted game of soccer</b></li><li class="class"><b>The footage emerged hours after a 'rebellion' broke out at the Altamira Regional Recovery Center in Brazil's northern Pará state at around 7am Monday</b></li><li class="class"><b>Gang members from one prison block invaded another and set a room on fire </b></li><li class="class"><b>At least 57 people have been killed - including 16 that where decapitated </b></li><li class="class"><b>Two correctional officers were held hostage during the riot and later released </b></li><li class="class"><b>Brazilian authorities have not named the two rival gangs involved in the attacks</b></li><li class="class"><b>The prison has a capacity of 200 detainees but was occupied by 311 prisoners</b></li><li class="class"><b>The bloody violence comes two months after a riot in Amazonas state jail left 55 inmates dead</b></li><li class="class"><b>WARNING: GRAPHIC CONTENT </b></li></ul><p class="author-section byline-plain">By <a href="/home/search.html?s=&amp;authornamef=Megan+Sheets+For+Dailymail.com" class="author" rel="nofollow">Megan Sheets For Dailymail.com</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/intent/follow?screen_name=@Megan__Sheets&amp;tw_p=followbutton" class="twitter-follow-author"><span class="follow-author"></span></a> </p><p class="byline-section"><span class="article-timestamp article-timestamp-published"> <span class="article-timestamp-label">Published:</span> 02:56 BST, 30 July 2019 </span> | <span class="article-timestamp article-timestamp-updated"> <span class="article-timestamp-label">Updated:</span> 04:41 BST, 30 July 2019 </span> </p><p></p><div data-preferred-shared-network-enabled="" id="articleIconLinksContainer"> <ul>

<span class="wai">e-mail</span> </a> </li> <li data-anchor="tl" data-twitter-status=" https://mol.im/a/7299563 via @MailOnline" data-formatted-headline="Gang members seen kicking decapitated heads amid Brazil prison battle" data-hide-email="true" data-article-id="7299563" data-article-channel-follow-button="MailOnline" data-is-channel="false" id="shareLinkTop" class="share-icons" data-placement="top" data-url="https://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-7299563/Video-Brazil-prison-battle-shows-gang-members-kicking-decapitated-heads-rivals.html"> <a class="js-sl share-link email_share_article-top" href="#socialLinks"></a> </li> </ul> <div class="share-count"> <b>104</b> <span>shares</span> </div> <a class="comments-count home" href="/news/article-7299563/Video-Brazil-prison-battle-shows-gang-members-kicking-decapitated-heads-rivals.html#comments"> <span></span> <p class="count-number"> 32</p> <p class="count-text">View <br /> comments</p> </a> </div> <!-- ad: https://mads.dailymail.co.uk/v4/sg/news/none/article/other/para_top.html --> <p></p><div itemprop="articleBody"><p class="mol-para-with-font">Sickening video from a bloody prison battle in Brazil shows twisted gang members playfully kicking the decapitated heads of their rivals on the roof of the jail as 57 people have been killed in the clash.   </p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Six or so inmates were seen horsing around on top of the Altamira Regional Recovery Center in Brazil's northern Pará state. </p><p class="mol-para-with-font">They appeared to be using human heads as balls for a sickening game of soccer.  </p><p class="mol-para-with-font">The footage emerged hours after a 'rebellion' broke out when gang members from one prison block invaded the prison annex and reportedly set part of it on fire around 7am. </p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Sixteen of the 57 dead were decapitated in the bloody five-hour-long clash that ended around midday, an official from the Para state government's penitentiary department said. </p><p class="mol-para-with-font">It was the latest violence to rock the country's overpopulated and deadly prison system.<span class="mol-style-bold"></span></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span class="mol-style-bold">WARNING: GRAPHIC CONTENT </span></p><div class="moduleFull mol-video"><div><div </div></div></div><p class="mol-para-with-font">Local reports said gang members from Block A stormed Block B, which was occupied by a rival group, locked a room and set it on fire, causing many prisoners to die of asphyxiation, as per the <a style="font-weight: bold;" target="_blank" class="class" rel="nofollow" href="https://observador.pt/2019/07/29/motim-faz-pelo-menos-52-mortos-em-prisao-do-brasil/">Oservador</a>.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Military police were called to the scene and negotiated with the inmates who had barricaded themselves in a cell block. </p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Brazilian media have reported that two prison officers were taken hostage in the conflict but were eventually freed following negotiations with civil police and the state's Prosecutor's Office. </p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Reported video of the conflict showed smoke billowing from one prison building. </p><div><div data-track-module="am-related_carousel^related_carousel" data-track-selector=".rotator-panels a:not([class*=external])" data-dm-rotator-rotate="false" data-track-pos="static" exactly two months after 55 people were confirmed dead in a riot in the northern Amazonas state of Brazil in May" class="blkBorder img-share" /> </noscript> </div> <p class="imageCaption">The riot comes exactly two months after 55 people were confirmed dead in a riot in the northern Amazonas state of Brazil in May</p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font">The Altamira prison has a capacity of 200 inmates but was occupied by 311 prisoners, according to Brazilian News outlet G1. </p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Brazilian authorities have not named the two rival gangs involved in the attacks.  </p><p class="mol-para-with-font">A fight between crime organizations would have motivated the rebellion, according to Brazilian newspaper<a style="font-weight: bold;" target="_blank" class="class" rel="nofollow" href="https://oglobo.globo.com/brasil/rebeliao-em-presidio-de-altamira-no-para-deixa-ao-menos-52-mortos-23839894"> O Globo.</a>  </p><p class="mol-para-with-font">However, violence in Brazilian prisons, particularly among gangs, is not uncommon. </p><p class="mol-para-with-font">The riot comes exactly two months after 55 people were confirmed dead in a riot in the northern Amazonas state of Brazil in May. </p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Monday's battle marked the second largest prison massacre in 2019.  </p></div>
            <!-- ad: https://mads.dailymail.co.uk/v4/sg/news/none/article/other/inread_player.html -->
